    --override root/cpu/cpuid=0 (Uns32) (default=0) (default) Set a unique ID for this CPU. The processor can read this value using impProcessorId() from simulatorIntercepts.h
    --override root/cpu/debugflags=0 (Uns32) (default=0) (default) Pass this debug value to the model (The model must be coded to accept it).
    --override root/cpu/mips=1.000000e+02 (Double) (default=1.000000e+02) (default) Specify the MIPS rate of this processor (in MHz)

# root/cpu/gdb
    --override root/cpu/alternategdbflags=(null) (String) (default=(null)) (default) Additional command-line flags for the gdb connected to this processor
    --override root/cpu/alternategdbpath=(null) (String) (default=(null)) (default) override the default path to the gdb connected to this processor
    --override root/cpu/gdbcommandfile=(null) (String) (default=(null)) (default) specify a file to be a read by a gdb connected to this processor
    --override root/cpu/gdbinit=(null) (String) (default=(null)) (default) tell gdb to execute this file before the prompt is displayed

# root/cpu/trace
    --override root/cpu/trace=1 (Boolean) (default=F) (override) Enable instruction tracing.
    --override root/cpu/tracebuffer=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Enable 256-entry trace buffer
    --override root/cpu/tracechange=1 (Boolean) (default=F) (override) Turn on the trace of register changes
    --override root/cpu/tracecount=0xffffffffffffffff (Uns64) (default=0xffffffffffffffff) (default) Trace for this many instructions
    --override root/cpu/tracehighpc=0xffffffffffffffff (Uns64) (default=0xffffffffffffffff) (default) Trace only instructions with this PC or lower
    --override root/cpu/traceintercept=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Trace calls of intercepted functions defined using processor ABI
    --override root/cpu/tracelowpc=0 (Uns64) (default=0) (default) Trace only instructions with this PC or higher
    --override root/cpu/tracemem=(null) (String) (default=(null)) (default) Print memory accesses by each instruction. Value is a string containing any of XSA, X=execute, S=system, A=read/write access
    --override root/cpu/tracemode=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Show the current processor mode when tracing instructions
    --override root/cpu/traceregsafter=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Print processor register contents after each instruction
    --override root/cpu/traceregsbefore=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Print processor register contents before each instruction
    --override root/cpu/traceshowcpuname=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Include the CPU name with every trace line including register and memory tracing
    --override root/cpu/traceshowicount=1 (Boolean) (default=F) (override) Include a per-processor instruction count in the trace output
    --override root/cpu/tracestart=0 (Uns64) (default=0) (default) Turn tracing on after this many instructions
    --override root/cpu/tracewrite=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Trace register writes even if the value does not change

# root/cpu/simulate
    --override root/cpu/maxinstructions=0xffffffffffffffff (Uns64) (default=0xffffffffffffffff) (default) Limit the maximum number of instructions to be executed before simulation ends
    --override root/cpu/startaddress=0x00000080 (Uns64) (default=0) (override) Set the PC to start at this specified address instead of using the hardware reset value, or the address found in the loaded program

# root/cpu/Fundamental
    --override root/cpu/Smepmp_version=1.0 (Enumeration) (default=1.0) (default) Specify required Smepmp Architecture version
    --override root/cpu/add_Extensions= (String) (default=) (default) Add extensions specified by letters to misa.Extensions (for example, specify "VD" to add V and D features)
    --override root/cpu/add_Extensions_mask= (String) (default=) (default) Add extensions specified by letters to mask of writable bits in misa.Extensions (for example, specify "VD" to add V and D features)
    --override root/cpu/add_implicit_Extensions= (String) (default=) (default) Add extensions specified by letters to implicitly-present extensions not visible in misa.Extensions
    --override root/cpu/enable_expanded=F (Boolean) (default=F) (default) Specify that 48-bit and 64-bit expanded instructions are supported
    --override root/cpu/endian=none (Endian) (default=none) (default) Model endian
    --override root/cpu/endianFixed=1 (Boolean) (default=F) (override) Specify that data endianness is fixed (mstatus.{MBE,SBE,UBE} fields are read-only)
    --override root/cpu/misa_Extensions=0x901106 (Uns32) (default=0x901106) (override) Override default value of misa.Extensions
    --override root/cpu/misa_Extensions_mask=0 (Uns32) (default=0) (default) Override mask of writable bits in misa.Extensions
    --override root/cpu/misa_MXL=1 (Uns32) (default=1) (default) Override default value of misa.MXL
    --override root/cpu/priv_version=1.12 (Enumeration) (default=1.12) (override) Specify required Privileged Architecture version
    --override root/cpu/sub_Extensions= (String) (default=) (default) Remove extensions specified by letters from misa.Extensions (for example, specify "VD" to remove V and D features)
    --override root/cpu/sub_Extensions_mask= (String) (default=) (default) Remove extensions specified by letters from mask of writable bits in misa.Extensions (for example, specify "VD" to remove V and D features)
    --override root/cpu/sub_implicit_Extensions= (String) (default=) (default) Remove extensions specified by letters from implicitly-present extensions not visible in misa.Extensions
    --override root/cpu/user_version=20191213 (Enumeration) (default=20191213) (default) Specify required User Architecture version
    --override root/cpu/variant=CV32E40S (Enumeration) (default=CV32E20) (platform) Selects variant (either a generic UISA or a specific model)
